class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2 style="text-align: left;">Flux is the Gateway to Blockchain</h2></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_2 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><a href="https://zel.network/zel/"><strong>Flux</strong></a>\xc2\xa0is the cryptocurrency powering the Flux Ecosystem, including a massive decentralized computational network. Flux gives users both institutional and private control over their cloud infrastructure in a decentralized manner.</p>\n<p>Flux provides incentives for miners and\xc2\xa0<strong><a href="https://zel.network/fluxnodes/">FluxNode</a></strong>\xc2\xa0operators on the highly scalable Flux network and\xc2\xa0is the currency for buying resources and fueling transactions on our computational network called\xc2\xa0<a href="https://zel.network/flux/#flux"><strong>FluxOS</strong>.</a></p></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper style="text-align: left;">ZelCore &amp; ZelCore+</h2></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_4 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><span><a href="/zelcore/"><strong>ZelCore</strong></a> is a fully-featured digital asset wallet for everyone. Store and manage over 275 cryptocurrencies and assets, including up to 12 individual wallet addresses for each. </span></p>\n<p><span>ZelCore is a non-custodial wallet and does not store or transmit any personal data or recovery seeds, giving you full control over your accounts, wallets, and private keys. Remember: <em><strong><span style="color: #36c9a5;">\xe2\x80\x9cNot your keys, not your crypto.\xe2\x80\x9d</span></strong></em></span></p>\n<p><span><strong><a href="/zelcore-2/">ZelCore+</a></strong> is the Premium version of <strong><a href="/zelcore/">ZelCore</a></strong>. With it, you have access to premium features including\xc2\xa0<span style="font-weight: 400;">additional wallet addresses, trading on built-in exchanges, node monitoring, and more.</span><br/> </span></p></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_3_wrapper et_pb_module">\n<a class="et_pb_button et_pb_button_3 et_pb_bg_layout_dark" created a scalable and decentralized network of computing power to run containerized applications through Docker.</span></p>\n<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><strong><a href="/zelnodes/">FluxNode</a></strong> Operators supply dedicated computing power, which generates revenue in Flux for powering the network.</span></p>\n<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><strong><a href="/flux/">FluxOS</a></strong> coordinates the deployment of dApps, manages available resources, and communicates between FluxNodes to provide real-time computing metrics.</span></p></div>\n</div> which can leave accounts vulnerable to attacks, such as SIM swapping and data breaches.</span></p>\n<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><strong><a href="/zelcore/">ZelCore</a></strong> uses the power of blockchain to offer a </span><b><i>Decentralized</i></b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> two-factor authentication. Secure your ZelCore account with d2FA, </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">which stores and verifies your encrypted PIN on the blockchain.</span></p>\n<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A protocol href="https://zel.network/zel/"><strong>Flux</strong></a>\xc2\xa0is the cryptocurrency powering the Flux Ecosystem, including a massive decentralized computational network. Flux gives users both institutional and private control over their cloud infrastructure in a decentralized manner.</p>\n<p>Flux provides incentives for miners and\xc2\xa0<strong><a href="https://zel.network/fluxnodes/">FluxNode</a></strong>\xc2\xa0operators on the highly scalable Flux network and\xc2\xa0is the currency for buying resources and fueling transactions on our computational network called\xc2\xa0<a href="https://zel.network/flux/#flux"><strong>FluxOS</strong>.</a></p></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_7_wrapper et_pb_module">\n<a class="et_pb_button et_pb_button_7 et_pb_bg_layout_dark" href="/zel/">read more</a>\n</div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_column --><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_16 et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">\n<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_5">\n<span class="et_pb_image_wrap"><img alt="ecosystem compresed" class="wp-image-6911" height="auto" loading="lazy" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 518px, 100vw" src="https://zel.network/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ecosystem-resized.gif" srcset="https://zel.network/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ecosystem-resized.gif 518w, https://zel.network/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ecosystem-resized-480x478.gif 480w" title="ecosystem-resized" width="auto"/></span>\n</div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_column -->\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_row --><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_11">\n<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_17 et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">\n<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_13 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h1>ZelCore &amp; ZelCore+</h1></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_14 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><span><a href="/zelcore/#zelcore"><strong>ZelCore</strong></a> is a fully-featured digital asset wallet for everyone. Store and manage over 275 cryptocurrencies and assets, including up to 12 individual wallet addresses for each. </span></p>\n<p><span>ZelCore is a non-custodial wallet and does not store or transmit any personal data or recovery seeds, giving you full control over your accounts, wallets, and private keys. Remember: <span style="color: #36c9a5;"><em><strong>\xe2\x80\x9cNot your keys, not your crypto.\xe2\x80\x9d</strong></em></span></span></p>\n<p><span><strong><a href="/zelcore-2/#zelcore+1">Zelcore+</a></strong> is the Premium version of <strong><a href="/zelcore/#zelcore">ZelCore</a></strong>. With it, you have access to premium features including\xc2\xa0additional wallet addresses, trading on built-in exchanges, node monitoring, and more.<br/> </span></p></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_8_wrapper et_pb_module">\n<a class="et_pb_button et_pb_button_8 et_pb_bg_layout_dark" href="/zelcore/">read more</a>\n</div>\n</div> <!-- et_pb_column_19 et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">\n<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_15 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h1>FluxNodes &amp; FluxOS</h1></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_16 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><span>We created a scalable and decentralized network of computing power to run containerized applications through Docker.</span></p>\n<p><span><strong><a href="/nodes/zelnode1">FluxNode</a></strong> Operators supply dedicated computing power, which generates revenue in Flux for powering the network.</span></p>\n<p><span><strong><a href="/flux/#flux">FluxOS</a></strong> coordinates the deployment of dApps, manages available resources, and communicates between FluxNodes to provide real-time computing metrics.</span></p></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_text et_pb_text_18 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">\n<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><span>Most traditional apps use centralized two-factor authentication (2FA)</span><span>, which can leave accounts vulnerable to attacks, such as SIM swapping and data breaches.</span></p>\n<p><span><strong><a href="/zelcore/#zelcore">ZelCore</a></strong> uses the power of blockchain to offer a </span><b><i>Decentralized</i></b><span> two-factor authentication. Secure your ZelCore account with d2FA, </span><span>which stores and verifies your encrypted PIN on the blockchain.</span></p>\n<p><span>A protocol that is truly seamless, secure, and private.</span></p></div>\n</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_10_wrapper et_pb_module">\n<a class="et_pb_button et_pb_button_10 et_pb_bg_layout_dark"
